style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >你在施展这道法术时能够发射至多相当于你威力值一半的飞弹数。以施法检定进行攻击，若你取得任一成功数，飞弹将对目标直接造成</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >点严重伤害，这属于纯粹的能量伤害。如果你射出多颗飞弹，你可以决定让所有飞弹攻击同一个目标也可以决定让飞弹射向不同目标，但每颗飞弹只能击中一个生物。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#160;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >无论目标是否有隐蔽、掩蔽（除非全掩蔽或全隐蔽）或是在近战中，飞弹都会精确命中目标。你不能指定飞弹攻击生物的特定部位。你可以用它攻击体积不大于</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >2</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >的独立物体（比如飞在空中的手雷），但被人持有的物品视为非独立物体。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#160;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-weight:bold;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >增幅</font></span></b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >：每额外支付</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >3</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >点魔力，飞弹的伤害就增加</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >点。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#160;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >：法术升阶，法术推演</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#160;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >法术等级达到</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >C</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >级时，该法术更名为</font></span><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-style:italic;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >飞弹风暴</font></span></i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >。</font></span><span >给手中的箭矢，弹药或者投掷武器注入魔力，让它们获得在你的意志指引下，向目标飞去。你可以对枪械施展这个法术，但只有这轮射出的第一发子弹会受到这个法术的作用。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-weight:bold;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >对抗</font></span></b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >：意志</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#160;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >施法者引导古老梦神的力量进入别人的心中，让他逐渐陷入昏睡。这个法术只能影响非超自然生物（进行了</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >C</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >级或以上血统强化的轮回小队成员同样视为超自然生物）。这个法术的咒语并不用以清晰响亮的方式念出来，而可以用近乎呢喃的声音悄悄念出，但这声音会像催眠的语言一样，直接在受影响的生物心中响起。如果法术成功，那么对方会忘记这件事情，失败的话则会立即发现异常。你在智力和学识上的每个附加成功以及施法者等级的每一级，可以使检定的难度提升</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >点。这道法术的效果在施展的过程中逐步生效。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#160;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#183;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >第一轮：法术的目标需要通过难度为威力值的意志检定，如果他在此检定中胜出，则法术立即结束，失败则感到昏昏欲睡，在先攻、防御和所有检定上承受等于失败数的表现减值。视当时的情况，目标的意志检定将获得加值或减值。例如，想在白天想让一个训练有素的精锐卫兵入睡，对方可在意志检定上获得</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >+2DP</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >加值，而对于一个连续带团三四天没有睡觉的</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >ST</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >，他将在对抗时承受</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >-2DP</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >减值。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#160;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#183;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >第二轮：目标需要再次通过难度为威力值的意志检定（此时他会承受之前的检定失败所带来的减值），如果失败则立即倒地沉睡。此时他处于神智不清的浅梦之中，任何人都可以通过一个成功的标准动作将他唤醒。若目标在此检定中胜出，他可以免于昏睡的效果，但依旧会因之前的失败而在法术持续时间内承受减值。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#160;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >这是一个如同法术等级的、心灵来源的睡眠效果。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#160;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-style:italic;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >材料</font></span></i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >：沙子跟玫瑰花瓣。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#160;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-weight:bold;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >研发</font></span></b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >：法术升阶，法术推演</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#160;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >法术等级达到</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >C</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >级时，该法术能够影响超自然生物，但这类生物的每个血统等级可以在意志判定上获得</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >+1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >附加成功的表现加值。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#160;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >法术等级达到</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >B</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >级时，该法术变为</font></span><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-style:italic;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >睡魔之瞳</font></span></i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#160;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:12.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >护盾</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:12.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#160;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-weight:bold;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >类别</font></span></b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >：力场</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#160;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-weight:bold;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >等级</font></span></b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >：</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >D&#160;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-weight:bold;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >能耗</font></span></b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >：</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >点</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#160;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-weight:bold;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >成份</font></span></b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >：言语，姿势</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#160;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >：反射或标准；见描述</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#160;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >：个人</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#160;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-weight:bold;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >目标</font></span></b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >：自身</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#160;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-weight:bold;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >持续</font></span></b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >：即时或一轮；见描述</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#160;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-weight:bold;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >对抗</font></span></b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >：无</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#160;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >这是贝尔卡式法术中最基本的战斗法术，因为如此常用，很多魔导师将这个法术登录在他们的魔导器中，作为常备的防护力来使用。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#160;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >你可以使用一个反射动作，以响应某次攻击的方式施展此法术。你的手上展开由光纹组成的魔法阵（圆形或旋转的三角形），阻挡攻击。对于你所响应的这一次攻击，此法术使你在防御和对抗范围效果的判定上获得威力值的掩蔽加值，并提供每</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >3</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >威力</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >点物理伤害吸收。这些是力场效果。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#160;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >如果你愿意，你可以挡在别人身前，以此用此法术同时为你和一个与你相邻的人防御。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#160;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >你也可以使用标准动作并消耗</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >意志，在维持全防御姿态的同时施展此法术，若你如此做，此法术的效果持续一轮，提供的物理伤害吸收变为全伤害吸收，且上升至每</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >2</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#160;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >将自己的眼球当魔法物品处理，变成固定魔术回路（类似魔术刻印的方法），将本用于接收外界讯息这种被动的机能，转化成主动影响外界事物的能力，但人工魔眼只能做到魅惑、暗示、强化而已。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#160;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >由于完成工程后获得的魔眼种类是确定的，因此你在学习这道法术时，只能选择一种常见的魔眼类型。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#160;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >魔眼在被使用时将发出红色或绿色的光，而高等级魔眼的颜色会变化为金色甚至虹色，若</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >ST</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >同意，你也可以自行设定更为特殊的颜色。这道法术无法其他获得超自然视觉的法术共存，并且在生效时会暂时占用你的瞳术位，使你已经具有的瞳术暂时失效。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#160;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-style:italic;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >魔眼工程</font></span></i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >的升阶效果因魔眼而异，但无论种类如何，以人工方式获得的魔眼究竟并非天生，因此只能升阶至</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >A</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >级。然而，在法术等级达到</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >A</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >级之后，你可以尝试将其固化。通过一个一小时的仪式，将魔术回路永固在你的瞳孔中，作为代价，你失去这道法术和</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >10</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >点魔力上限。若如此做，你永久获得一个瞳术强化，这个瞳术的名称如同你选择的魔眼，等级为</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >A</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >级，且不再被视为法术，但不会改变你获得的属性加值。除此以外，这个瞳术的效果与增幅到上限的该法术效果完全相同。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#160;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:12.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >魅惑魔眼</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1</span><span >看到你眼睛或被你看到的人容易被你诱导控制。在法术的持续时间内，你在对他人进行社交类判定时所有互动系技能均视为已受训而不受惩罚。此外，你对他人进行的操控相关检定获得威力值</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:12.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >强化魔眼（千里眼）</font></span><span style="text-align:left;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >强化你眼睛的基本能力，使动态视力增强。在法术的持续时间内，你的视距比原先扩展一半，并在攻击和防御上获得威力值的洞察加值。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#160;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >DR/</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#160;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-weight:bold;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >持续</font></span></b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >：立即</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#160;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-weight:bold;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >对抗</font></span></b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >：强韧（物品）</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#160;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >以自身为媒介，将神圣的能量引导入绝对纯净的水中，就可以制造出这种被称为天使之泪的圣水。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#160;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >这一炼造过程需要</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >小时的持续工作，并消耗法术材料。在施展这道法术后，每十分钟你都需要进行一次施法检定，这是难度为</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >10</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >的延长动作。若一小时后尚未取得足够多的成功数，则炼制失败。如果成功，圣水就被制造出来。此时再进行一次施法检定，决定圣水的效力。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#160;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >若将其保存在瓶中，它不会挥发和变质，可以永久的保存下去。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#160;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >一整瓶圣水可以作为一件</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >0B</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >的投掷武器使用，以接触攻击命中生物时不造成通常的伤害，而是使瓶中的圣水溅出至</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >5</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >米内的所有生物。圣水对非黑暗生物不会产生任何效果；然而，黑暗生物一旦沾上圣水，就会受到如同制造成功数的伤害，这些伤害属于纯粹的正能量。被命中的黑暗生物可以进行强韧检定来对抗这个伤害，每个成功数可以抵消</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >点，但承受如同威力值的神圣减值。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#160;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >圣水也可以以一个移动动作洒在武器或防具上，这个用法被称为祝圣。一把祝圣武器将获得</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >[</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >光明</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >]</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >特性，并额外增加威力值的破魔，而一件祝圣防具会获得</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >DR/</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >黑暗和负能量抗力，数量相当于威力值的一半。这种使用方式可以持续</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >轮</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >成功数。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#160;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-style:italic;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >材料</font></span></i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-weight:bold;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >对抗</font></span></b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >：无</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#160;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >你可以凝聚自然界中与自身魔力凝练而成的元素，使其在你的身边成形，在你的指令下向目标飞射而出。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#160;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >施展法术时，你必须在灼热，寒冷，电击，腐蚀中选择一种能量做为伤害类型。或者，你也可以使用穿刺伤害作为伤害类型。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#160;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >你以施法检定进行一次远程能量武器射击，向目标射出一支能量箭。能量箭的伤害在法术强度的基础上获得威力值的能量加值。由于击发的速度极快，因此有着高速优势</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >5</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#160;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >D</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >级以上的每个施法者等级，你可以额外支付</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >2</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >点魔力，使</font></span><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >级（单发射击</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#8594;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#160;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >作为施法的一部分，你将</font></span><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-style:italic;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >魔法射手</font></span></i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >缠绕在自己的近战武器或天生武器上，并立刻以该武器发动一次攻击，但是施法时间提升为一个整轮动作。这次攻击中武器的伤害获得额外的加值，相当于魔法射手能量箭的伤害数，并能获得对应的高速优势，造成的伤害中不超过武器伤害的部分可以转为能量箭所造成的伤害类型。以这种方式使用该法术时依旧能进行增幅，但不会提高速射等级。你可以通过后续的拓展研究强化这种用法：</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#160;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >法术等级达到</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >C</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >级时，你可以额外投入</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >DD+750</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >或等量经验，使你能发动两次攻击而不是一次。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#160;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >级时，你可以额外投入</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >C+1000</span><span ><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="text-align:left;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:12.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >围绕施术者，出现水晶般的透明防壁，法阵和咒字在上面显现。这些防壁不会阻碍你的任何行动，但是可以自动抵挡攻击。你在念诵的时候必须将魔导书打开置于手上，并进行施法检定以决定效果的强弱。</font></span><span >你获得了威力值的掩蔽防御加值，并在对所有范围效果的对抗判定上获得同一加值，这视为掩蔽效果。同时防壁为你提供了法术等级的能量抗力，可以吸收除腐蚀效果之外的所有种类能量伤害。晶壁可以转化利用它吸收的能量，每吸收</font></span><span
